================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/VCH_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → VCH Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/VCH_Tahoe/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → VCH Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/VCH_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → VCH Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Coastal_Health/VCH_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Coastal Health → VCH Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/Ladder_Truck/Body/Ladder/weldLadderServer.server.lua ---

--[[
    weldLadderServer (Script)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → Ladder Truck → Body → Ladder
    Parent: Ladder
    Properties:
        Disabled: false
        RunContext: Enum.RunContext.Legacy
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local platform = script.Parent.Parent.Parent.Chassis.Platform;
local platformCFrame = platform.CFrame;

local L1 = script.Parent.Ladder.L1
local L1WeldPart = L1.L1Weld;

local L2 = script.Parent.Ladder.L2
local L2WeldPart = L2.L2Weld;

local L3 = script.Parent.Ladder.L3
local L3WeldPart = L3.L3Weld;

local LadderBase = script.Parent.Parent.LadderRotation;

local horizontalBase = script.Parent.HPivot;
local horizontalPivot = script.Parent.HPivot_1;

local verticalBase = script.Parent.VPivot
local verticalPivot = script.Parent.VPivot_1;

local base = script.Parent.Base;

local seat = script.Parent.Seat;

local newInstance = Instance.new;

local descendants = script.Parent:GetDescendants();


function weldParts(part0, part1, parentToPart0)
	local newWeld = newInstance('Weld');
	newWeld.Part0 = part0;
	newWeld.Part1 = part1;
	newWeld.C1 = part1.CFrame:Inverse() * part0.CFrame;
	newWeld.Parent = script.Parent.WeldStorage;
	if parentToPart0 then
		newWeld.Parent = part0;
	end
end

weldParts(verticalBase, horizontalPivot);
weldParts(LadderBase, horizontalBase);
weldParts(seat, horizontalPivot);
weldParts(L1WeldPart, verticalPivot)
weldParts(L2WeldPart, L1WeldPart, true);
weldParts(L3WeldPart, L2WeldPart, true);
weldParts(base, horizontalPivot);

for _,v in next, L1:GetDescendants() do
	if v:IsA('BasePart') or v:IsA('UnionOperation') then
		if v.Name ~= 'L1Weld' then
			weldParts(L1WeldPart, v);
		end
	end
end

for _,v in next, script.Parent.Ladder.BaseDesign:GetDescendants() do
	if v:IsA('BasePart') or v:IsA('UnionOperation') then
		weldParts(v, horizontalPivot);
	end
end

for _,v in next, L2:GetDescendants() do
	if v:IsA('BasePart') or v:IsA('UnionOperation') then
		if v.Name ~= 'L2Weld' then
			weldParts(L2WeldPart, v);
		end
	end
end

for _,v in next, L3:GetDescendants() do
	if v:IsA('BasePart') or v:IsA('UnionOperation') then
		if v.Name ~= 'L3Weld' then
			weldParts(L3WeldPart, v);
		end
	end
end

for _,v in next, script.Parent:GetDescendants() do
	if v:IsA('BasePart') or v:IsA('UnionOperation') then
		v.Anchored = false;
	end
end

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → Ladder Truck → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local T1 = elsModule(ELSModel.T1);
	local T2 = elsModule(ELSModel.T2);
	local T3 = elsModule(ELSModel.T3);
	local T4 = elsModule(ELSModel.T4);
	local G1 = elsModule(ELSModel.G1);
	local G2 = elsModule(ELSModel.G2);
	local G3 = elsModule(ELSModel.G3);
	local G4 = elsModule(ELSModel.G4);
	local S1 = elsModule(ELSModel.Parent.Ladder.Ladder.L3.S1);
	local E1 = elsModule(ELSModel.E1);
	local E2 = elsModule(ELSModel.E2);
	local S3 = elsModule(ELSModel.S3);
	local S4 = elsModule(ELSModel.S4);
	local S5 = elsModule(ELSModel.S5);
	local H1 = elsModule(ELSModel.H1);
	local H2 = elsModule(ELSModel.H2);
	if enabled then
		while true do	
			T1(0);
			T2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
			T3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
			T4(0);
			G1(1);
			G2(1);
			G3(1);
			G4(1);
			S1(0);
			E1(0);
			E2(0);
			S3(0);
			S4(1);
			S5(1);
			H1(0);
			H2(0);
			wait(0.15);
			
			T1(1);
			T2(1);
			T3(1);
			T4(1);
			G1(1);
			G2(1);
			G3(1);
			G4(1);
			S1(1);
			E1(1);
			E2(1);
			S3(1);
			S4(1);
			S5(1);
			H1(1);
			H2(1);

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/Ladder_Truck/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → Ladder Truck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/Ladder_Truck/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → Ladder Truck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/Ladder_Truck/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → Ladder Truck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/Ladder_Truck/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → Ladder Truck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/Ladder_Truck/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → Ladder Truck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;

local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	
	-- LIGHTBAR
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1);
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2);
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3);
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4);
	local F5 = elsModule(ELSModel.F5);
	local F6 = elsModule(ELSModel.F6);
	local F7 = elsModule(ELSModel.F7);
	local F8 = elsModule(ELSModel.F8);
	local F9 = elsModule(ELSModel.F9);

	-- Front Lights
	local M1 = elsModule(ELSModel.M1);
	local M2 = elsModule(ELSModel.M2);
	local M3 = elsModule(ELSModel.M3);
	local M4 = elsModule(ELSModel.M4);

	-- Door Lights
	local G1 = elsModule(ELSModel.G1);
	local G2 = elsModule(ELSModel.G2);

	-- Tiny Lightbar Lights
	local A1 = elsModule(ELSModel.A1);
	local A2 = elsModule(ELSModel.A2);
	local A3 = elsModule(ELSModel.A3);
	local A4 = elsModule(ELSModel.A4);

	-- Back Lights
	local C1 = elsModule(ELSModel.C1);
	local C2 = elsModule(ELSModel.C2);
	local C3 = elsModule(ELSModel.C3);
	local C4 = elsModule(ELSModel.C4);
	local C5 = elsModule(ELSModel.C5);
	local C6 = elsModule(ELSModel.C6);
	local C7 = elsModule(ELSModel.C7);
	local C8 = elsModule(ELSModel.C8);

	-- Back Lights (actual back)
	local X1 = elsModule(ELSModel.X1);
	local X2 = elsModule(ELSModel.X2);
	local X3 = elsModule(ELSModel.X3);
	local X4 = elsModule(ELSModel.X4);
	
	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					F1(1);
					F2(1);
					F3(1);
					F4(1);
					F5(1);
					F6(1);
					F7(1);
					F8(1);
					F9(1);
					wait(0.1);
				end
			end)
		end)()
			coroutine.wrap(function()
				pcall(function()
					while true do
						M1(1);
						M2(1);
						M3(1);
						M4(1);
						wait(0.1);
						M1(1);
						M2(1);
						M3(1);
						M4(1);
						wait(0.1);
				   end
			    end)
			end)()
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					G1(0);
					G2(1);
					wait(0.05);
					G1(1);
					G2(1);
					wait(0.05);
					G1(1);
					G2(0);
					wait(0.05);
					G1(1);
					G2(1);
					wait(0.05);
				end
			end)
		end)()
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					A1(1);
					A2(1);
					A3(1);
					A4(1);
					wait(0.1);
					A1(1);
					A2(1);
					A3(1);
					A4(1);
					wait(0.1);
				end
			end)
		end)()
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					C1(1);
					C2(1);
					C3(0);
					C4(0);
					C5(1);
					C6(1);
					C7(0);
					C8(0);
					wait(0.2);
					C1(0);
					C2(0);
					C3(1);
					C4(1);
					C5(0);
					C6(0);
					C7(1);
					C8(1);
					wait(0.2);
				end
			end)
		end)()
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					X1(1);
					X2(0);
					X3(0);
					X4(1);
					wait(0.15);
					X1(0);
					X2(1);
					X3(1);
					X4(0);
					wait(0.15);
				end
			end)
		end)()
	else
		X1(1);
		X2(1);
		X3(1);
		X4(1);
		C1(1);
		C2(1);
		C3(1);
		C4(1);
		C5(1);
		C6(1);
		C7(1);
		C8(1);
		A1(1);
		A2(1);
		A3(1);
		A4(1);
		G1(1);
		G2(1);
		M1(1);
		M2(1);
		M3(1);
		M4(1);
		F1(1);
		F2(1);
		F3(1);
		F4(1);
		F5(1);
		F6(1);
		F7(1);
		F8(1);
		F9(1);
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/Pump_Truck/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → Pump Truck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/Pump_Truck/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → Pump Truck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/Pump_Truck/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → Pump Truck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/Pump_Truck/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → Pump Truck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/Pump_Truck/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → Pump Truck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;

	local M2 = elsModule(ELSModel.M2);
	local M3 = elsModule(ELSModel.M3);
	local M4 = elsModule(ELSModel.M4);

	-- Door Lights

	local G2 = elsModule(ELSModel.G2);

	local C2 = elsModule(ELSModel.C2);

	local X3 = elsModule(ELSModel.X3);
	local X4 = elsModule(ELSModel.X4);
	
	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					F1(1);
					F2(1);
					F3(1);
					F4(1);
					F5(1);
					F6(1);
					F7(1);
					F8(1);
					F9(1);

				end
			end)
		end)()
			coroutine.wrap(function()
				pcall(function()
					while true do
						M1(1);
						M2(1);

						M4(1);
						wait(0.1);
						M1(1);
						M2(1);
						M3(1);
						M4(1);
						wait(0.1);
				   end
			    end)
			end)()
		coroutine.wrap(function()

					G1(0);

					G2(1);
					wait(0.05);

					wait(0.05);
					G1(1);
					G2(1);
					wait(0.05);
				end
			end)
		end)()
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					C1(1);
					C2(1);
					C3(0);
					C4(0);
					C5(1);
					C6(1);
					C7(0);
					C8(0);
					wait(0.2);
					C1(0);
					C2(0);
					C3(1);
					C4(1);
					C5(0);
					C6(0);
					C7(1);
					C8(1);
					wait(0.2);
				end
			end)

		coroutine.wrap(function()

	else

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/Rescue_Truck/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → Rescue Truck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/Rescue_Truck/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → Rescue Truck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end

	121

    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/Rescue_Truck/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → Rescue Truck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/Rescue_Truck/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → Rescue Truck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/Tech._Rescue_Truck/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → Tech. Rescue Truck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/Tech._Rescue_Truck/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → Tech. Rescue Truck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/Tech._Rescue_Truck/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → Tech. Rescue Truck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/Tech._Rescue_Truck/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → Tech. Rescue Truck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/Tech._Rescue_Truck/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → Tech. Rescue Truck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/VFRS_BC_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → VFRS BC Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/VFRS_BC_Tahoe/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → VFRS BC Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/VFRS_BC_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → VFRS BC Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/VFRS_BC_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → VFRS BC Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/VFRS_Chief_Explorer/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → VFRS Chief Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/VFRS_Chief_Explorer/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → VFRS Chief Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/VFRS_Chief_Explorer/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → VFRS Chief Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/VFRS_Chief_Explorer/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → VFRS Chief Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/VFRS_F-350/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → VFRS F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/VFRS_F-350/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → VFRS F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/VFRS_F-350/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → VFRS F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/VFRS_F-350/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → VFRS F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				if v:FindFirstChild('Attachment') then
					v.Attachment.Light.Enabled = true;
				else
					v.Light.Enabled = true;
				end
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				if v:FindFirstChild('Attachment') then
					v.Attachment.Light.Enabled = false;
				else
					v.Light.Enabled = false;
				end
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			if v:FindFirstChild('Attachment') then
				v.Attachment.Light.Enabled = false;
			else
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/VFRS_HM18/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → VFRS HM18 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/VFRS_HM18/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → VFRS HM18 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/VFRS_HM18/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → VFRS HM18 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/VFRS_HM18/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → VFRS HM18 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/VFRS_HM18/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → VFRS HM18 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local T1 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.T1);
	local T2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.T2);
	local T3 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.T3);
	local T4 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.T4);
	local F1 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.F1);
	local F2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.F2);	
	local S1 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.S1);
	local S2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.S2);
	local S3 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.S3);
	local S4 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.S4);	
	if enabled then
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					F1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));				
					F2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
					T1(0);
					T2(0);
					T3(0);
					T4(0);
					S1(0);
					S2(0);
					S3(1);
					S4(1);
					wait()

				end
			end)
		end)

	else
		T1(1);
		T2(1);
		T3(1);
		T4(1);
		S1(1);
		S2(1);
		S3(1);
		S4(1);
		F1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));				
		F2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));			
	end
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/VFRS_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → VFRS Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/VFRS_Sprinter/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → VFRS Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/VFRS_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → VFRS Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights2;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		body.Headlights.Logo.Material = neonMaterial
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		body.Headlights.Logo.Material = smoothMaterial
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/VFRS_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → VFRS Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Fire_Rescue_Service/VFRS_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service → VFRS Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:50
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;
